It is also quite possible there will be more than one recession during this hot zone period (July 
2026–March 2031), as this time band will coincide with the balsamic phase of the Saturn–Uranus 
cycle. The balsamic phase of a planetary cycle covers the last 45° (waning semi-square) and is asso-
ciated with a time when the dynamics of the cycle are usually in conflict. It is a time when the col-
lective realizes something is coming to an end. Matters of importance just aren’t working anymore, 
and something new has to begin. It’s a Pluto-like period, even though Pluto is not involved in the 
Saturn–Uranus balsamic period. But, as shown in the prior chapter, transiting Pluto at 3°–7° Aquarius 
is intensely involved with the Sun–Moon opposite Uranus in the Chart of Mankind (3°–7° of the 
fixed signs Taurus–Scorpio).
Historically, the balsamic phase of the Saturn–Uranus cycle has relevance to the world and 
national economy, as multiple recessions often happen in this relatively short period, especially when 
near the onset of the waning semi-square. Saturn and Uranus will be in their last 45° waning semi-
square phase from April 12, 2027, through January 12, 2028, though the entire balsamic period will 
last until summer 2032, when the two planets conjoin each other. The economy tends to struggle 
slightly before and during the semi-square time, but usually recovers smartly by the arrival of the 
conjunction, which will take place on June 28, 2032. 
As described in last year’s book, “… the last two times these two planets were in their waning 
semi-square aspect to one another were 1981-1982 and 1937. These were painful secondary reces-
sions to the even more serious recession depths of 1974 and 1932, respectively. The economy strug-
gled during these periods but then recovered sharply going into—or coming out of—the conjunction. 
I expect the same this time, given the overlap of these cycles in 2026-2031.” But the point remains 
that there may be more than one recession during this five-year period, as there were in the balsamic 
phases of 1981–1988 and 1937–1942.
Last year’s book also highlighted a third geocosmic cycle related to the economy of the near 
future: the Jupiter–Saturn cycle. Here is how that cycle works. The economy and global stock market 
cycles tend to perform well within one year of the 20-year conjunction between Jupiter and Saturn. 
Then, as they approach their waxing semi-square two to three years later, there is a financial and 
military crisis. This is usually followed by a strong economy and stock market occurring during the 
third through the sixth years after their conjunction. But then, in years seven to nine, there is a more 
serious economic and financial crisis heading into the Jupiter–Saturn opposition. 
In current terms, the Jupiter and Saturn synodic (conjunction) cycle began on December 21, 
2020. There was a financial and military crisis that erupted in 2022–2023. The “growth” part of the 
cycle is now in effect from 2023 to 2026. However, the seven- to nine-year period of an economic 
and stock market crisis is due 2027-2030, which overlaps with both the Saturn–Neptune conjunction, 
Saturn–Uranus waning semi-square, and the Lunar North Nodal cycle described above. They all 
overlap in the year 2027, which is the “sweet spot” for a recession. But these potential events related 
to long-term geocosmic cycles can have an orb of up to one year on either side.

﻿THE FEDERAL RESERVE BOARD:
A FIGHT FOR CONTROL
RE VIEW AND PREVIEW
The Bureau of Labor Statistics says the U.S. job market is much weaker than initially believed. 
More than 900,000 fewer jobs were added in 2024 and 2025 than previously reported. The BLS 
issues revisions every year, but this change is the biggest on record and comes after President 
Trump fired the BLS commissioner after a weak monthly jobs report.
—Geoff Bennett, “Revised Job Numbers Raise New Concerns About Economic Slow-
down,” PBS NewsHour, YouTube, September 9, 2025.
Last year’s Forecast 2025 book correctly identified major challenges the Federal Reserve Board 
would encounter with the U.S. government. It stated, “Saturn (on the MC) is the demand, and Nep-
tune is the impracticality, the unrealism of the expectations to be met. Hampering the Fed at the same 
time is the fact that the Saturn–Neptune conjunction squares the Fed’s Sun. It’s not sure what to do. 
The Sun is the Chair of the Fed. If things go wrong, he is especially vulnerable to being a scapegoat, 
the person blamed. The Saturn–Neptune also squares Pluto in the 12th house of hidden enemies, of 
those who are doing reputational harm for a hidden agenda. So, we may have a case where someone, 
or some entity, is slandering the Fed or its Chair as part of a maneuver to gain power and control of 
the nation’s central bank by eliminating the Chair or the institution (bank) itself.”
The book went on to correctly state, “The situation is compounded when you look at the transit 
of Pluto (the terminator) on the FRB’s natal Uranus (independence). It is happening near the 8th 
house cusp, which (like Pluto) has an astrological dynamic of termination. The message here is that 
a powerful force may try to take away the independence of the Fed and do so in a very underhanded 
and deceptive manner.”
And finally, last year’s book concluded, “If a drama unfolds similar to that just described here, 
it will coincide with the bottom of the Aries Vortex abyss. It would be an epic struggle between the 
government and its central bank, probably between the president and the chairman of the Federal 
Reserve Bank…. The Fed needs to be very careful as it enters this period where its reputation, cred-
ibility, and even its existence may be on the line. It will need to fight to defend its reputation.” And 
this is just about the way it happened.
Right from the beginning of his second term, President Trump threatened to remove FRB Chair 
Jerome Powell, even before his term had ended. The only problem was that he could not legally do 
so. Instead, he began replacing Fed governors who resigned with governors who would carry out 
his agenda. He has threatened to fire others and replace them with governors who will carry out his 
wishes to lower interest rates. It is a bold political move to take increasing control of the nation’s 
central bank. Indeed, the Fed’s independence is at risk. In fact, its very existence may be at risk.

Figure 8: Transits (outer circle), February 20, 2026, to the Federal Reserve Board chart (inner circle).
TRANSITS TO ITS FOUNDING CHART
The Federal Reserve Act was signed into law by President Woodrow Wilson. The New York 
Times edition of December 24, 1913, reported that the Federal Reserve was created on December 23, 
1913, at 6:02 PM, in Washington, D.C. According to its own website, www.federalreserve.gov, “It 
was created by Congress to provide the nation with a safer, more flexible, and more stable monetary 
and financial system.” Basically, it does this by managing two mandates: inflation and unemploy-
ment. Its job is to keep both low, and by doing so, the economy supposedly functions well.
Those two functions are currently in conflict with one another. The labor market has not been 
growing as robustly in 2025 as it was in 2024. Part of the problem was that the Bureau of Labor 
Statistics underreported by more than 900,000 the number of jobs that were added in 2024 and 
2025 than previously stated. The economy and labor market were not nearly as strong as thought, 
and subsequent reports supported that view. Hence, the Fed believed it was more important to 
stimulate the economy by starting a new round of lowering its benchmark Fed funds rate in the 
last quarter of 2025. This meant it was willing to risk that inflation would increase, even though 
## Page 82

78
it never fell to its preferred target of 2%. As rates fell, inflation began to creep up to 3% as this 
is being written. The Fed is now stuck—perhaps confused is a better word—as to what course of 
action to take. Does it continue to provide stimulus to a slowing economy with lower rates, as 
President Trump wishes? Or does it resume its fight to control inflation by raising rates? Or do 
nothing and see what happens?
The transit of Saturn in hard aspect to natal points in the Fed chart indicates times of tighten-
ing or raising rates. Jupiter transits show when the Fed is in a more accommodative mood to lower 
rates and stimulate the economy. Neptune also leans toward lower rates but is often associated with 
poor judgment, uncertainty, or an unwillingness to take any action, one way or the other, regarding 
rate adjustments. 
The Aries Vortex finds both Saturn and Neptune conjoining on the Midheaven (MC) of the Fed 
chart and making a T-square to its Sun–Pluto opposition, while Jupiter transits back and forth over 
its Mars and Ascendant in opposition to its own Jupiter. This perfectly describes the Fed’s dilemma 
as we enter 2026. Jupiter wants to lower rates, Saturn wants to fight inflation, and Neptune isn’t sure 
what to do, for focusing on one part of its dual mandate means putting the other part at risk. In the 
meantime, the power struggle with the Executive Office continues to mount, with Saturn (authority 
and control) in hard aspect to Pluto (power).
Transiting Jupiter will continue crisscrossing the Fed’s Ascendant and Mars, and opposing its 
Jupiter, through May 2026. That is when Jerome Powell’s tenure as Fed Chair ends. However, his 
term as a Fed governor continues until January 31, 2028. Will Trump terminate his role as Fed gover-
nor then as well? The Federal Reserve Act allows the president to remove members of the board only 
“for cause.” In June 2026, Jupiter (exaggeration and overacting) will conjoin the Fed’s natal Neptune, 
the planet of uncertainty and confusion. There is likely to be a lot of confusion after his term ends as 
Fed Chair. It should get very interesting as we approach that period in 2026.
The drama doesn’t end, however, as 2026 finds transiting Pluto (coercion and force) conjoining 
the Fed’s natal Uranus (independence). This aspect comes within minutes of an exact conjunction in 
April–June 2026, before hitting its exact point with three conjunctions between February and Decem-
ber 2027. If the Fed is going to lose its independence, this might be the time. In fact, since an 18-year 
stock market cycle trough is due then—during which the DJIA could lose 35–65% from its all-time 
high—and the U.S. economy is in the Lunar Nodal cycle for a deep recession, the threat (or reality) 
of loss to the Fed’s independence could be the cause of a financial panic around that time. With Pluto, 
reforms and resolutions to conflicts are seldom easy. Yet reform and resolution to long-standing prob-
lems are the explanations offered for why the government has to take such draconian actions. With 
Pluto, change usually comes with a considerable amount of pain to the masses. 
In the meantime, Jupiter (accommodation) is in harmonious aspect to Mercury and Venus in the 
Fed’s chart in September 2026, so there may be another rate cut around that time. Saturn will also 
trine Mercury from June 2026 through March 2027, so there may be some stability then. However, it 
won’t dominate the powerful Pluto transit in conjunction with Uranus in the Fed’s chart, underlining 
the effort to possibly end the Fed’s independence.

﻿THE UNITED STATES IN 2026:
EXCEPTIONALISM VERSUS STATUS DOWNGRADE
American exceptionalism is an idea that the United States of America is a unique and even 
morally superior country for historical, ideological, or religious reasons. Proponents of Amer-
ican exceptionalism generally pair the belief with the claim that the United States is obligated 
to play a special role in global politics. 
—Adam Volle, “American Exceptionalism,” www.brittanica.com.
The past week I’ve talked to two historians, one rightish, one leftish, and both conversations 
turned toward Thomas Jefferson’s stinging bill of particulars against King George III in the 
Declaration of Independence. They resonate in unexpected ways: “For cutting off our Trade 
with all parts of the world.” “He has excited domestic insurrections amongst us.” “He has 
kept among us, in times of peace, Standing Armies without the Consent of our Legislatures.” 
“He has erected a multitude of New Offices, and sent hither swarms of Officers to harass our 
people.” “Obstructing the Laws for Naturalization of Foreigners; refusing to pass others to 
encourage their migration hither.” The Founders didn’t want any of that. It’s why they created 
a republic. 
—Peggy Noonan, “A Republic, But Can We Keep It?” www.wsj.com, October 24, 2025.
REVIEW OF 2025
Last year’s book, written in October-November 2024, well before Donald Trump’s second term 
in office began on January 20, 2025, correctly pointed out many of the issues that the nation would 
face. 
The book began with an overview of the nation’s military challenges. It stated: “Mars, in a 
nation’s chart, rules its military. In a hard aspect from a progressed planet, it symbolizes perceived 
threats to the nation that could result in the deployment of its military. Is it to defend the nation 
against external threats? Possibly, as Mars is in the 9th house of foreign lands. Could it relate to 
domestic disturbances? That is possible, too, for Mars in the 9th house also relates to protesters, 
especially in colleges and universities.” The book went on to state, “….the president (could) take 
action that may involve the National Guard or military in 2025-2026 …. The progressed Sun (leader) 
in Pisces means the president will try to attain peace. But Mars in the 9th house may indicate others 
are in the mood to resist or fight him.” 
One of the most notable events of last year was the United States’ bombing of Iran in mid-June. 
This was done in order to stop Iran’s nuclear program, which posed an existential risk to Israel. Iran’s 
nuclear program was thus set back several years. Last year’s book specifically stated, “This same 
progressed aspect also brings into play the Mars-Neptune square in the chart of Iran. Thus, tensions 
between Iran and the United States may reach a point of crisis. This may be a time when the U.S. 
military is tested to see just how prepared and competent they are in handling foreign aggression.”
On the economy, last year’s book stated, “…progressed Venus is separating from its opposition 
to progressed Saturn near the cusps of the 2nd and 8th houses and applying to a favorable sextile to 
Jupiter in Cancer. This may bode well for the Treasury.” The U.S. Treasury set a record for revenues 
received, according to the U.S. Treasury Fiscal Data. This should have helped balance the budget and 
## Page 84

80
cut back the deficit. Unfortunately, the outlays of funds exceeded the record revenues received, so the 
debt and deficit continued to increase despite record tax receipts.
Still regarding the economy and financial matters, last year’s book pointed out, “But as they 
(Saturn and Neptune) straddle the Pisces-Aries boundary between March 2025 and February 2026, 
they will form a challenging waning square to the U.S. natal Venus in Cancer. This might be a time of 
financial crisis or a threat to the nation’s central bank (the Federal Reserve Bank). The government 
may be very critical of the central bank and even demand more authority in their decision-making…. 
March 2025-February 2026 may be a very tense period between the Fed and the president.” Indeed, 
there was a brief financial crisis in early April 2025 when the president announced his “Liberation 
Day” tariffs, calling for new and high tariffs on other countries, even America’s allies. The president 
also tried to fire Fed Chair Jerome Powell and Fed Governor Lisa Cook, as he began making strides 
to insert new governors onto the Fed’s board who would carry out his wish for lower interest rates.
Overall, the U.S. economy did well in 2025 as this is being written in mid-October. Employment 
is still growing, though at a slower pace than the previous year. The nation has continued to assert its 
dominance in military matters throughout the world, but particularly in the Middle East, where the 
president brokered the historic Gaza Peace Plan between Israel and Palestine in October. And ille-
gal immigration into the country is down significantly. These are all positives in the minds of most 
Americans, which relates to last year’s geocosmic analysis.
Yet the nation continues to face many familiar and new formidable issues as it enters 2026. The 
partisanship of politics continues to be divisive and not unifying. The nation’s debt continues to rise, 
and corporations have become reluctant to hire new people and invest heavily in research and product 
development due to the nation’s uncertain trade policies. The new tariff policies are effectively a tax 
on businesses that import and will eventually result in higher costs for goods and services redirected 
onto consumers. The nation is now witnessing the deployment of its military and National Guard into 
several major cities at the direction of the president, and against the will of the leaders and citizens of 
those states. The president has commenced a retribution/revenge initiative against his opponents after 
campaigning on the promise that he would not do so, that his success would be his revenge. But law-
fare has indeed taken over much of the Justice Department’s duties, not to mention absorbing much 
of the daily headlines of news outlets. Protests against the style of government, allegations of cor-
ruption, violations of basic ethical principles, and money-grabbing by leaders of the administration 
are rising. This is leading to increased anxiety about the direction the nation is headed. The nation’s 
populace is in a sour mood as it begins the new year, despite claims to the contrary by the White 
House and MAGA. According to The Hill (October 22, 2025, www.thehill.com), “6 in 10 Say U.S. 
Headed in Wrong Direction.” The number is actually 62%, according to the article. In short, despite 
its success enhancing national security, the nation is experiencing growing anxiety and uncertainty 
about its future in the eyes of its citizens.
Is the U.S. really a republic supported by principles of democracy and a government for the peo-
ple, of the people, and by the people, which has long been the view that has led to the idea of Ameri-
can exceptionalism for over two centuries? Or is it turning into an authoritarian regime where the 
people are coerced into accepting the dictates of the president and his followers without their consent 
or representation? There is even a question as to whether or not the Executive Branch has subsumed 
too many of the roles traditionally belonging to Congress. In short, the question arises: Does the idea 
of American exceptionalism continue to exist? And if so, in what form? Or is it changing form?

THE CHART OF THE UNITED STATES
“High tariffs inevitably lead to retaliation by foreign countries and the triggering of fierce 
trade wars,’’ Ronald Reagan said. “The result is more and more tariffs, higher and higher 
trade barriers, and less and less competition. So, soon, because of the prices made artificially 
high by tariffs that subsidize inefficiency and poor management, people stop buying. Then the 
worst happens: Markets shrink and collapse; businesses and industries shut down; and mil-
lions of people lose their jobs.’’ 
—Ronald Reagan, as quoted from a radio address given April 25, 1987, written by Paul 
Wiseman, “Trump Says a Canadian Ad Misstated Ronald Reagan’s Views on Tariffs. 
Here Are the Facts and Context,” AP News (apnews.com), October 24, 2025.
As noted in the annual Forecast book over the past several years, I use July 2, 1776. Previously, I 
had also used 11:50 AM in Philadelphia as the time of the founding chart of the U.S. for two reasons. 
First, it fits the history of when the vote for independence was taken, and second, the chart works 
well from an astrological viewpoint. However, no one really knows the exact time, or even day, the 
United States actually completed the vote for its independence. Yet due to the vast changes initiated 
in the United States in 2025, I am adjusting the time of its inception by 35 minutes earlier, to 11:15 
AM. I am rectifying the time to 11:15 AM because that will give the U.S. a 0° Libra rising. Given that 
the Aries Vortex involving Saturn and Neptune is conjunct at 0° Aries, and the Uranus–Pluto trine 
midpoint is also at 0° Aries, I think this slightly adjusted chart with those outer planet placements 
highlighting the 0° cardinal signs on the angles, aligns more closely with the events and changes that 
are occurring at this time in the United States.
The new time still fits within the realm of possibilities as to when the vote for independence was 
completed. We know that the vote—the decision of the new nation to declare itself independent—was 
completed on July 2, 1776, according to David McCullough, historian, and author of the book 1776.1 
And according to astrologer Gary Noel, in a discussion in the ISAR e-zine (www.isarastrology.org) 
several years ago, it is likely that the vote took place before noon because it was announced in the 
evening newspaper. In order to make the evening edition of the daily news, articles had to be submitted 
before noon. So 11:15 AM is still close but before noon, as was our previously used time of 11:50 AM. 
The adjustment in time does not change the position of the planets relative to their signs. They 
remain the same. Libra is still rising, which means Venus still rules the chart, but it is now even 
stronger than before as it resides right on the midheaven at 0° Cancer. This might make the case for 
America’s exceptionalism based on democracy, fairness, and the idea that “all men are created equal” 
even stronger. This revised chart still finds Saturn rising in Libra, where it is exalted, representing 
the importance of laws that are fair and policies that support equal rights for all citizens, which are 
also characteristics that have defined the view of exceptionalism often ascribed to the United States. 
However, these virtues are now being questioned by others both within and outside the U.S. as Saturn 
and Neptune transit the new descendant.

THE U.S. PROGRESSED CHART—WAR VERSUS DIPLOMACY 
We start our analysis of the United States in 2026 by analyzing the secondary progressions to the 
founding chart. The date chosen for the progressed chart is July 2, 2026, which would be the 250th 
birth date of the nation.
There is one clear planetary configuration that shows up in this chart. July 2026 will find the 
nation undergoing a progressed new moon, with both the Sun and Moon conjoining at 19° Pisces. A 
progressed new moon represents a new beginning in the life of the nation, especially when it aspects 
other planets in the natal or progressed chart, which just happens to be the case here. That is, the pro-
gressed new moon will be in an exact square to Mars of the founding chart. Furthermore, it sets off 
the Mars-Neptune mutable square in the U.S. chart in a configuration known as a mutable T-square, 
with the focal planet being Mars at 19° Gemini in the nation’s 9th house of education, courts of law, 
religion, trade, and foreign affairs. 
The most important parts of this pattern involve these planets, for they represent the actions of the 
nation, or the choice of whether to act or not when faced with issues that have a Mars theme (anger, 
threats, war). With natal Mars in Gemini, chances are the nation will commence a multitude of many 
new activities. This is further highlighted by the fact that these planets are in mutable signs, which 
means the nation is multitasking—performing several operations or tasks at once. The challenge will 
be to stay focused on one matter at a time, not to get distracted by too many conflicting demands, and 
to do a complete and thorough job with each issue it takes on. The temptation is to spread itself so 
thin that nothing seems to be completed adequately enough to please everyone. Everything is hurried. 
Mistakes and misjudgments occur.

conflict, forcing Hamas to surrender and return hostages to Israel. These were great examples of Mars 
in action, displaying strength in order to achieve peace, which is the positive way these principles can 
be integrated. In these instances, the U.S. garnered respect and admiration throughout the world. 
In other cases, such as the Russian-Ukrainian conflict, the U.S. approach has taken a more Pisces-
Neptunian course. First, the U.S. would not support Ukraine in its war with Russia. Then it said it would, 
then backed off and decided it wanted to help resolve the conflict through diplomacy, in which neither 
nation was willing to give up anything. So, what is the criterion under which the U.S. decides to be the 
aggressor versus when it decides to be the peacemaker? Under what conditions will the U.S. defend its 
allies, and when not? No one knows. The progressed New Moon in Pisces is making a mutable T-square to 
the Mars-Neptune square in the U.S. founding chart, exhibiting this lack of consistency in policy involving 
international conflicts. But the New Moon in Pisces strongly suggests that it wants to find a peaceful path 
utilizing diplomacy. Yet that only works when all parties are sincerely interested, which, in this case, with 
Mars as the midpoint of this T-square, is clearly not happening between Russia and Ukraine.
Another feature of this progressed New Moon in Pisces, forming a mutable T-square to the U.S. 
natal Mars-Neptune square, is that it continues to activate the mutable Mars-Neptune square of Iran’s 
chart over the next three years. The conflict with Iran is not likely to end with the June 2025 bomb-
ing of its nuclear sites. That conflict is probably just dormant for now and will come back again. The 
U.S. must be ready.
It is also important to remember that the U.S. progressed Mars is retrograde. That started shortly 
after Barack Obama became president (2008-2009). It will continue through 2087. Astrologically, 
this progressed retrograde Mars poses a problem of readiness for the U.S. military, especially as it is 
in Libra, its detriment. The U.S. leadership will have to be very alert to avoid mistakes, miscalcula-
tions, and dangerous indecisiveness when clarity and firmness are needed for success. It also indi-
cates conducting war campaigns only partway, not seeing them through to needed completion. As a 
result, war successes may have to be entered into a second time with the same actors. The ongoing 
conflict with Iran may be an example of this.

2043. On April 12, 1861, just one day before the 164-year orbital cycle of Neptune entered Aries, the 
U.S. Civil War commenced. Neptune next entered Aries on March 30, 2025. After retrograding back 
into Pisces, it will re-enter Aries on January 26, 2026, where it will remain until 2038. Uranus has 
an 84-year orbital cycle and had previously entered Gemini on August 7, 1941. Four months later, 
the U.S. entered World War II. It entered Gemini again on July 7, 2025. After retrograding back into 
Taurus, it will re-enter Gemini on April 26, 2026, and remain there through August 3, 2032. As we 
advance through 2026 and into 2027, Uranus, Neptune, and Pluto will all be in their first decan (10°) 
of these same signs, where they were posited during the most important wars in American history. 
This is clearly a war cycle for the U.S. Can it avoid a war this time?

NATIONAL AND LOCAL SECURITY 
Almost every issue of importance confronting the United States today can be associated with 
the Aries Vortex, where the Saturn–Neptune conjunction falls on the U.S. descendant and squares 
its natal Venus (chart ruler) on the midheaven. It also pertains to the Uranus–Pluto trine in early air 
signs, which makes up the sides of the funnel, and whose midpoint also falls on 0° Aries with Saturn 
and Neptune. Additionally, transiting Uranus and Pluto make a grand trine to the early Libra rising in 
this newly rectified chart.
Let us start with the issue of trust, an important factor in the status of America’s exceptionalism. 
Trust falls under the domain of Neptune. But Neptune is compromised via its conjunction with Sat-
urn, which is not trust, but rather skepticism, which can easily turn to distrust and even separation if 
one of the parties in a relationship feels that the agreement or precedents supporting the relationship 
are being changed without its approval and consent. Relationships are the key to this current chart 
because the Saturn–Neptune conjunction is on the cusp of the 7th house, which rules partnerships and 
allies. Furthermore, both Saturn and Neptune square the U.S. Venus in Cancer. Venus also rules one’s 
partnerships and allies, those who support the nation and have been loyal to it. 
All of this support and trust has been upended since March, when first Neptune, and then Sat-
urn, moved into Aries, forming these powerful aspects to the U.S. chart. The White House suddenly 
announced huge tariffs on nations that export its goods to the U.S. Aside from causing a mini-panic 
in financial markets in early April (Venus rules the stock market), this abrupt disruption of long-
standing precedence in trade and international relationships has led many of the U.S. allies to seek 
other nations to fill in the gap of lost trade relations with the U.S. It’s not like they completely stopped 
trading with the U.S., for developing new alliances and trading partners take time. But these changing 
trade relationships are underway as we enter 2026, for many nations no longer trust the U.S. to honor 
its precedents. They fear (Saturn) that abrupt, non-consensual changes can and will happen again, and 
in many cases, may be due to some act or statement on their part that personally offends the President. 
This is perhaps the leading reason why America is losing its status of exceptionalism in the eyes of 
the world. It takes a long time to build up trust. It takes only a moment to break it. Without trust, you 
do not have the foundation for a healthy relationship. America has now jeopardized its relationship 
with many of its historic allies. It will be interesting to see if it can recapture that trust before those 
other nations develop new trading alliances.
The consequences of these heavy-handed unilateral trade decisions have also led the charge for 
the currencies of other multinational alliances (like BRICS) to compete with the U.S. Dollar as an 
acceptable standard world currency for trade. Again, this relates to the nation’s Venus being besieged 
by Saturn and Neptune. Venus represents a nation’s currency, and the U.S. Dollar has been falling in 
value as of January 2025. It has declined to a new 3-year low as of this writing.
Despite these challenges indicated by Saturn and Neptune, the transits of Uranus and Pluto, 
making a grand trine with this revised U.S. Ascendant, hold much promise. The U.S. is still a world 
leader in technology and innovation. With Uranus transiting back to its natal sign of Gemini, this 
techno-renaissance is likely to continue. More discoveries and new applications with technology 
are forecasted throughout this decade, and especially in 2026. However, Uranus in Gemini has also 
corresponded to deadly wars for the U.S. in every past instance. Technology and innovation have led 
to economic booms, but in many cases, these discoveries and applications were brought about due 
to war entanglements. This might actually help the U.S. in its military campaigns, but there is still 
## Page 92

88
the issue of a progressed Mars retrograde, which points out the tendency to not end these conflicts 
completely, but rather just conduct a temporary “shock and awe” strike, followed by a break that lets 
the nation’s adversaries regroup to fight another day.
The nation’s economy might continue to hold up and even improve somewhat while transiting 
Jupiter is in Cancer, where the U.S. natal Sun, Venus, and Jupiter are located. It has already passed 
those natal planets as of August 2025, which could mean the peak of the economy has passed. How-
ever, Jupiter will still conjoin Mercury from October 2025 through June 2026. During the early 
stretch of that time, Jupiter will also trine Saturn, from October 2025 to January 2026. This may be a 
secondary economic peak.
New challenges begin to arise as Saturn advances past Neptune in Aries. It will move from its 
square to Venus to a waning square to the U.S. Jupiter and Sun for about one year, starting in March 
2026. This portends new struggles with the economy, world trade, and the leadership of the country 
(Sun), losing the support of its citizenry. The White House believes it will retain control of the House 
and Senate as it has worked hard to redraw voting districts in order to enhance its chances of gaining 
seats. But Saturn will square the nation’s Cancer planets, and Jupiter, leaving its Sun sign during next 
year’s election season, does not support that belief. With Neptune on the descendant, square natal 
Venus, a ploy to interrupt the normal election process cannot be ruled out. Accusations of cheating or 
stealing are likely to be made again.
In conclusion, it appears the United States starts out the year on a strong footing, but not as 
strong as it was prior to August 2025. But as the first quarter of 2026 ends, it also appears that ten-
sions increase with regard to both the economy, trading partners, and the overall direction of the 
U.S. leadership. The U.S. mid-term elections of 2026 hold the potential of another bout of national 
anxiety, division, and allegations of fraud, stealing, and cheating. Such is the lot of Neptune and 
Saturn, prominent as transits in hard aspect to critical points in the U.S. founding chart. At the same 
time, the U.S. is on track to make major advancements in technology and space exploration. It’s not 
as if everything is in decline. Some matters are improving and doing quite well, especially in these 
areas. One other area of concern may be health matters. In this regard, it is not just the U.S., but many 
other nations of the world that need to be alert to the possibility of new contagions erupting under the 
Saturn–Neptune conjunction.

Today marked an extraordinary inflection point in time for the Middle East as President Don-
ald Trump signed the historic Gaza Peace Deal alongside world leaders. President Trump’s 
strategy of ‘peace through strength’ brokered a historic peace agreement that stands to bring to 
an end a conflict that has ravaged the Middle East and perpetuated the spread of terrorism… 
Their work, under the leadership of President Trump, represents the most significant peace 
agreement in the Middle East since the end of the Second World War. 
—Press release of RSC (Republican Study Committee), “President Trump’s Triumph for 
Peace in the Middle East,” October 13, 2025, rsc-pfluger.house.gov.
“Speak softly but carry a big stick. You will go far.” If Roosevelt were alive today, he might 
caution our current government not to forget the “speak softly” part. As he defined it, it is nec-
essary to be respectful toward all people and scrupulously refrain from wronging them. While 
at the same time keeping ourselves in position to prevent wrong being done to us. 
—Brett Baier, “To Rescue the American Spirit: Teddy Roosevelt and the Birth of a Super-
power,” Mariner Books, 2025
Writing about President Donald Trump is a challenge, no matter how objective one may try to 
be. If his accomplishments are noted in a positive light, far-left partisans will charge you with being a 
MAGA (Trump-supporting) extremist. If you point out his ill-advised decisions and potentially harm-
ful actions to the nation or the world, you are afflicted by TDS—Trump Derangement Syndrome—
according to MAGA extremists. “Ill-advised decisions and actions” is probably an incorrect phrase, 
anyway, for the president has many advisors who try to give him good advice. However, he often acts 
without their input or consent. He creates many problems that did not exist and that only he can solve. 
True to his Gemini cosmic heritage, he plays the roles of villain and then hero.
Thus, as challenging as it is to write this section of the book as someone without bias and subjec-
tivity, I will nevertheless attempt to do so.
THE NATAL CHART
According to published copies of his birth certificate, Donald Trump was born on June 14, 1946, 
at 10:54 AM, in Queens, NY. 
He was born under a powerful lunar eclipse with the Sun conjunct Uranus in Gemini and the Moon 
in Sagittarius. He has been called a genius and unorthodox, which are traits associated with the Sun and 
Uranus in Gemini. But he has also been called chaotic and a disruptor, which are also terms associated with 
this combination. The Moon in Sagittarius has a very large vision of what is possible and, with the Sun in 
opposition, can indicate unbridled confidence in himself and an unwavering demand of loyalty from oth-
ers to serve that vision, and even himself as a leader. He wishes complete freedom in whatever he does. 
He was also born with Mars conjunct the Ascendant in Leo. In fact, his late Leo rising is conjunct 
Regulus, the fixed star of “royalty and the height of power and wealth.” Is it any wonder that he is 
often accused of “acting like a king?” But with Mars there as well, he will oftentimes act impulsively, 
do what he wants, and not take the time or effort to follow any protocol or normal procedure.

What we have seen this year is new levels of graft and grift. We seem to be moving rapidly

The next major transit unfolding will be Saturn forming a cardinal T-square to the President’s

onto others, which they assert is a result of his own actions or thoughts. This is a classical Mercury-

begin to increase.

fact that it is not allowed in the Constitution as it now stands. But the Lunar North Node entering the 
lower part of his chart suggests he also sees value in winding down and not complicating his legacy 
by forcing the Constitution to change, and the negative reactions that may cause.

 THE DOW JONES INDUSTRIAL AVERAGE (DJIA) IN 2026
by Raymond Merriman
As the saying goes, don’t mistake a bull market for brains… Remember, no one rings a bell at 
the top or bottom of the market, but there are faint sounds. 
—Andy Kessler, “The ‘Don’t Worry, Be Happy’ Market,” The Wall Street Journal, 
November 3, 2025.

INTRODUCTION
The U.S. stock market has been on a tear for the past 17 years, following its 72-year cycle low of 
March 6–9, 2009, at the height of the Great Recession, when the DJIA had dropped 54.4% from its 
then all-time high made just 17 months earlier, in October 2007. The low in March 2009 was 6470 in 
the DJIA. By the end of October 2025 (as this is being written), it was trading at a new all-time high 
of 48,040, a gain of over 742% in 16.5 years, which isn’t bad. It demonstrates how wealth is built in 
the stock market via knowledge of investing and cycle studies during long-term cycle troughs. 
Along the way, however, there have been seven cases of 16% or greater declines in the DJIA, 
with the steepest being the 37% one-month decline from February 2020 to March 2020, during the 
outbreak of the COVID-19 pandemic. That is a lot of steep sell-offs in just 18 years (2007–2025). 
They ranged in intervals of 1–4 years from one another as follows:
1. March 2009	
	
	
54.4% decline from high of October 2007
2. October 2011 (31 mo) 	
	
19.2% decline from high of May 2011
3. August 2015 (46 mo)	
	
16.2% decline from high of May 2015
4. December 2018 (40 mo)	 	
19.4% decline from the high of October 2018
5. March 2020 (15 mo)	
	
37.1% decline from high of February 2020
6. October 2022 (31 mo)	
	
22.4% decline from high of January 2022
7. April 2025 (30 mo)	
	
18.8% decline from high of December 2024
## Page 103

99
Of the seven completed cases of 16% or greater declines since the then all-time high of October 
2007, six have lasted 30–46 months. The outlier was 2020’s pandemic low at only a 15-month inter-
val. That was indeed an outlier in many ways. If the next 16+% decline happens in the 30–46 month 
interval, it would occur from October 2027 to February 2029. As will be demonstrated shortly, that 
falls within the time band of several cycles, including the important 18-year cycle trough, a genera-
tional low that is due 2022–2030. 
Yet, when one looks at the long-term history of the DJIA (as illustrated in The Ultimate Book on 
Stock Market Timing, Volume 1: Cycles and Patterns in the Indexes 1), the picture is concerning, because 
1) the low to a high in the 18-year cycle has lasted 6–20 years in all 12 completed cases to date, and 2) 
in 11 of those 12 cases, the rally lasted 9–20 years. As 2026 begins, it will mark the 17th year that this 
cycle has been overall bullish, which makes it in the mature stage of its 18-year cycle. The peak of the 
18-year cycle is due at any time now, followed by the low, which is also due any time by 2030.
Historically, though, the crest has been 17 years or greater in three of those 12 cases, for only a 
25% frequency. However, all three cases of these short but steep declines have occurred within the 
four cases since the Great Depression of 1932, which was the prior 72-year cycle. This means bull 
markets have lasted 17–20 years in 75% of the four most recent cases. This will be the 4th time in 
the last five cases that it has lasted at least 17 years, and three of the prior four bull runs have lasted 
18–20 years. The cycle top is due. 
It’s as if you know you are this close, but also that far away, from an important top, after which 
the stock market historically falls at least 37%. The frequency of a 37% or greater decline happening 
by 2030 is about 83% (10 of 12 cases). And in eight of those cases, the decline was between 37.5 and 
63.6%. Only once was the decline less than 30% (in 1953). And only twice was it greater than 63.6%. 
Since this next 18-year cycle low is not expected to be part of a greater cycle, the range of 
37.5–63.6% is the projected drop off from the current all-time high that is due. If it falls more than 
63.6%, or even more than the 54.4% decline into the long-term cycle low of March 2009, then an 
even longer-term 90-year cycle must be considered. That degree of decline has only occurred twice in 
## Page 104

100
U.S. stocks: into the lows of 1842 and 1932. If the 90-year cycle is to occur a third time, it would be 
due within 15 years of 2022, and probably within 10 years of 2022 (by 2032), based on the long-term 
Saturn–Uranus conjunction taking place on June 28, 2032. Our studies have shown that the greatest 
percentage of long-term stock market cycles have occurred near a Saturn–Uranus conjunction or 
opposition than any other planetary pair cycle.1 
The takeaway from this introduction is that the DJIA is due to top out any time before 2029, 
and most likely between 2026 and 2029. However, there is just as strong a probability that the 
18-year cycle low will happen October 2027–January 2029, and the crest would happen before 
then. The challenge is: how much before then? Since 1932, there have been no bear markets at the 
end of the 18-year cycle that lasted more than two years. Two of them lasted less than one year. 
The shortest on record was the 40% decline in just two months from August to October 1987. It is 
this author’s opinion that under President Donald Trump, we will see another instance of a steep 
and brief bear market lasting less than two years, and probably less than one year. Nevertheless, a 
decline of 37–63% will offer a generational opportunity to build wealth via the stock market for 
those who are willing to be patient for 9–20 years afterwards, which could yield a return between 
300% and 800%.2
Now, let’s see if we can add more pieces of the current stock market puzzle in the quest to narrow 
the time band for both the crest and the trough. For if we can, that guidance can mean the difference 
between a very healthy and profitable investment on the horizon versus one that could be meager if 
entering at the wrong time (too early or too late) or one that could even spell a severe loss if not care-
ful and aware of the cycle messages ahead.
CYCLES: LONG-TERM
We begin this section with a review of long-term cycles (low to low) in the DJIA.
The 18-Year Cycle: The last 18-, 36-, and 72-year cycles started with the low of March 6–9, 2009. 
Our focus will be on the 18-year cycle, as that is the longest cycle currently coming due, from 2024 to 
2030. Since it is the first phase of longer cycles, it is not expected to be as steep a decline as happened 
into the low of March 2009, which was 54.4% in the DJIA. However, as noted earlier, over 80% of 
18-year cycles have declined 37–63%, so this remains our price target for this important cycle.
Time-wise, the crest is due any time before the end of 2029. The low will follow and is due at 
any time before the end of 2030. 
Historically, the price appreciation from the start of the 18-year cycle to its crest has been 122–
778%. However, since 1914, it has gained 320–778%. Measured from the start of the current cycle 
at 6470, the upside price target for the crest is 27,174–56,807. As of this writing, the DJIA is in the 
upper part of this range, nearing 50,000. Thus, the time and price criteria for the 18-year cycle crest 
are being met. The final high is due at any time.
The 9-Year Cycle: All cycles break down into divisions of 2 and 3, and sometimes both. The half-
cycle (9-year cycle) to the 18-year cycle has a range of 7.5–10.5 years. The 9-year half-cycle time band 
has coincided with a prominent trough in 10 of the 12 cases to date in the 18-year cycle, with some 
slight distortions. The March 2020 pandemic low, for instance, was exactly 11 years following the start 
of the 18-year cycle, and although slightly outside of our normal range, it will be considered a 9-year 
half-cycle. If correct, the second 9-year half-cycle is next due September 2027–September 2030.
## Page 105

101
Price-wise, in all but two of these cases, the crest of the second half of the 18-year cycle was 
considerably higher than the crest of the first half. That is the case again now. 
The 6-Year Cycle: The six-year cycle is a 1/3 division of the 18-year cycle. It has a normal range 
of 5–7 years, but can expand to eight years in the second or third phase. In all 12 cases of the 18-year 
cycle, there has been a 5–7-year cycle low in the first phase. However, the current 18-year cycle 
is now in its third phase. The first phase was a double bottom in August 2015 and February 2016, 
which was 6–7 years following the start of the cycle in March 2009. The second phase was the low 
on October 13, 2022, again 6–7 years after the first phase trough. Allowing a range of 5–8 years, the 
final phase will be due 2027–2030.
The measured price targets for the crest of this third 6-year cycle phase are 47,500 +/– 4842 
and 50,244 +/– 4115. The overlap is 46,128–52,342. Once completed, we will look for a decline of 
37–63%. We would also look for prices to fall to or below the 108-month moving average shown on 
the monthly chart.

Within the longer-term 9- and 6-year cycles, the DJIA also subdivides into two or three phases. 
The current 9-year cycle has been exhibiting three 3-year phases. The 6-year cycle can also be sub-
divided into two 3-year phases or three 2-year sub-cycles. Both share in common a 3-year cycle. 
This often happens with “combination cycles,” and this 18-year cycle is a combination of 9-year 
and 6-year cycle phases. They share in common a 3-year cycle with a range of 30–42 months, which 
MMA Analyst Ulric Aspegrén calls a “keystone cycle,” which means it is a subdivision of two in one 
cycle branch and a subdivision of three in another. 
It is for this reason that we will focus on the 3-year cycle and not the 4-year (or even 4.5-year) 
cycles of our longer-term studies. Besides, the three-year cycle has been more reliable than the 4-year 
cycle over the past 50 years. 
Following the 9-year cycle low of March 2020, the DJIA has exhibited 3-year cycle lows in Octo-
ber 2022 (31 months) and April 2025 (30 months). The April 2025 low was the second of three 3-year 
phases to the 9-year cycle. It was also the first of two 3-year cycles troughs that make up the 6-year 
cycle that began in October 2022. Thus, the next 3-year cycle low is on schedule to complete not only 
the 9- and 6-year cycles, but the entire 18-year cycle. If we measure 30–42 months following the low 
of April 7, 2025, we get an ideal time band for all four cycles (18-, 9-, 6-, and 3-year) due between 
October 2027 and October 2028. However, we have to be careful because when longer-term cycles 
are due, the shorter-term cycles (phases) within them can distort (contract or expand) beyond their 
normal time bands.
## Page 106

102
I began this chapter with the study of the seven declines of 16% or greater since the 72-year cycle 
crest of October 2007. To repeat, “Of the seven complete cases of 16% or greater declines since the 
then all-time high of October 2007, six have lasted 30–46 months. If the next 16+% decline happens 
in the 30–46 month interval, it would occur October 2027–February 2029.” It overlaps nicely with 
the 18-, 9-, 6-, and 3-year cycles.
Our formal studies on price gains and losses in The Ultimate Book on Stock Market Timing, Vol-
ume 1: Cycles and Patterns in the Indexes1 were conducted on 4–year cycles. However, since Table 2 
showed a 4-year cycle low that also began April 7, 2025, and its next low is also due during the 2028 
+/– 1 year time band, we can apply those studies to the current market and calculate a price target 
for the crest of all these cycles. First of all, these studies show that the vast majority of rallies from 
the low to the high of a 4-year cycle last 12–49 months with a price appreciation of 70–189%. This 
would mean that the crest will 1) likely occur after March 2026 and 2) could soar to 62,240–105,800. 
However, there is a caveat. This is the last 3-year cycle phase of 6- and 9-year cycles, which 
are in their last phase of the greater 18-year cycle. The percentage of appreciation in the last 4-year 
cycle phases of an 18-year cycle, in our formal studies, was not so great. It ranged from a gain of 
only 29% to 83% in six of the seven cases since 1893. That would yield an upside price target of only 
47,225–67,000. This is interesting because it overlaps with our measured upside price calculation of 
the 9-year cycle at 49,400–57,750 and the 6-year cycle at 51,609–56,481. Earlier, we calculated that 
the 18-year cycle crest would rise to 27,174–56,807, and the six-year cycle to 46,128–52,342. It may 
be too much to expect, but all four of these price calculations overlap 51,609–52,342. 
The final intermediate-term cycle we consider is the 50-week type, with a normal range of 34–67 
weeks. Usually, there will be three of these phases within a 3-year cycle. April 7, 2025, began the first 
50-week (and 3-year) cycle. It is due to bottom with 16.5 weeks of March 27, 2026, or December 1, 
2025–July 17, 2026. But this will only be the first of three 50-week cycles before the final 3-, 6-, 9-, 
and 18-year cycles come due. In fact, there could even be more or fewer than three 50-week phases 
here since this is the last stage of so many greater cycles converging, which is when distortions most 
often occur. The timing is never easy when very long-term generational bottoms unfold. Investors 
need to develop a buy-in plan whenever the DJIA falls more than 35% off its all-time high, which 
could begin as early as 2026.
For now, our immediate trading plan calls for a buying opportunity within 16 weeks of March 27, 
2026, and with a decline of at least 8%. Yet, if the next 50-week cycle rally only makes a double top 
to the high of this current 50-week cycle, or stalls within an upside price target range given above, 
investors must be prepared for a powerful reversal to begin.
GEOCOSMIC CYCLES
Our basic rule is that long-term cycle crests and troughs tend to unfold when major aspects 
involving long-term planetary pair cycles involving Saturn, Uranus, Neptune, or Pluto are in effect. 
We also consider the sign position of the Lunar North Node.
We have two long-term planetary pair cycles in effect now. First and foremost is the 36-year syn-
odic (conjunction) cycle of Saturn and Neptune, which came within 13’ of a degree of exactness in 
July 2025 and will be exact on February 20, 2026. Our studies reported in The Ultimate Book on Stock 
Market Timing Volume 2: Geocosmic Correlations to Investment Cycles2 showed that long-term stock 
## Page 107

103
market cycles tended to top out within 11 months of the beginning through the end of this aspect, with 
all but one in 8 months or less. This means the long-term cycle crest could happen by October 2026. 
The second long-term planetary aspect is Uranus trine Pluto, which will transpire five times 
between July 2026 and May 2028. It was close enough in the middle of 2025 to be considered already 
underway (less than a degree from an exact trine). There are only three cases of trines between these 
two planets in the history of the DJIA. Two of them were 9-year cycle troughs. With an orb of 10 
months on either side of the first or last passage, this fits well in a broad time band for the 18-year 
cycle as described previously. However, this is too wide a time band to be of any practical use. The 
Saturn–Neptune conjunction is more useful for identifying a possible 18-year cycle crest.
Both Saturn and Neptune will make sextiles to Uranus and Pluto in 2025–2026. This is a favor-
able combination that could also help identify a long-term cycle crest whose time band is now in 
effect. Saturn makes three sextiles from April 4, 2025, to March 28, 2026. Neptune will sextile Ura-
nus and Pluto from August 28, 2025, through June 6, 2027. The overlap of August 2025 through 
March 2026 stands out for an important reversal. It will likely be at least a 50-week cycle crest, but 
could also exhibit the first 50-week cycle trough.
There is also a very significant cosmic arrangement taking place July 20–21, 2026, as mentioned 
in our brief note to traders at the beginning of this year’s book. This is when Jupiter will trine Nep-
tune, oppose Pluto, and be in sextile to Uranus. Within six months, and usually only two, the Jupiter–
Neptune trine has a strong correlation to at least a 50-week cycle trough. The Jupiter sextile Uranus 
aspect is also similar to a propensity to identify a 50-week or greater cycle low within 4 months. 
However, the Jupiter/Pluto opposition is most important. It can be either an intermediate (or longer 
term) cycle low or high, or both, within six months. If it is a high, it takes place within only 4 months, 
and a powerful decline follows. This fits well with our outlook of the 18-year cycle crest unfolding in 
2026, and ideally within four months of July 2026.
The Jupiter–Saturn Cycle 
Throughout history, intermediate or long–term cycle highs and lows in the U.S. stock market 
have related to the 20-year Jupiter–Saturn cycle as follows: 
During the conjunction, stock markets tend to make highs.
1–3 years later, near the first 1/8 phase (waxing semi-square) of the 20-year cycle, the U.S. 
stock market completes an intermediate-term cycle low. There is usually an international military war 
breaking out then as well.
•	
The stock market tends to rally and form an important crest 3–6 years after the conjunction.
•	
The stock market tends to suffer a serious decline, even a crash, 7–9 years after the conjunction.
The Jupiter–Saturn conjunction occurred on December 20, 2020, and there indeed was a military 
crisis as the six-year stock market cycle trough occurred in October 2022 (1–3 years after the con-
junction). The market was then due to rally 3–6 years after that low, which brings us to 2023–2026, 
and indeed the market has rallied into this time band. The next step involves a serious decline, per-
haps a crash, into an important long-term cycle low due in 2027–2029. Once again, this aligns with 
the labeling of the long-term cycles according to the “Cycles Progress Table” given earlier. Our 
expectation is for the DJIA to lose 37–63% of its value from the high to the low during this period.
## Page 108

104
The Jupiter Sign Correlation
Jupiter will transit the sign of Leo from June 30, 2026, through July 26, 2027. A filtered wave of 
DJIA prices over the past 100+ years shows this to be a planet-sign combination with a strong ten-
dency for significant lows. Sometimes these declines last into the next sign of Virgo before the final 
low is completed.
The Lunar North Node Stock Market Cycle 
The transits of the Moon’s North Node through the signs also show a correlation to long-term cycle 
crests and troughs in the DJIA. Long-term cycle lows happen most frequently when the Moon’s North 
Node transits between 1° Aries and 10° Sagittarius. This will be in effect from December 2024 to October 
2030. However, these studies also show the greatest concentration of lows was when the Moon’s North 
Node transited between 18° Pisces and 29° Capricorn. This condition will be present from August 2025 
to April 2028. Note that this overlaps with our projection of the next 18-year cycle (2027–2029).
November 2026 through April 2027 stands out because Jupiter will be in Leo, in opposition to the 
Lunar North Node in Aquarius. Both correlate to long-term cycle lows in the DJIA. The hard opposition 
between these two might time this low, or at least a significant leg down to the final 18-year cycle low. 
Figure 16: Moon’s Nodes through the signs and their correspondence to the U.S. stock market. Long-
term cycle lows in the U.S. stock market happen mostly between 1° Aries and 10° Sagittarius, with the 
greatest concentration between 18° Pisces and 29° Capricorn (shown in the shaded area marked “low”).

THE U.S. POLITICAL CYCLE
The possibility of new all-time highs in 2025–2026, followed by a very sharp decline into 2027–
2029, is also shown by the correlation of stock market crashes to the party in office, as described in 
the last two years’ Forecast books. 
In the past 120 years, all but one major stock market “crash” has happened under a Republican 
president. And the one that happened under a Democratic presidency in 1966 was the least severe of 
all (26.5%). At the same time, all-time highs were achieved under every Republican president since 
1900. However, that has not been the case under three Democratic presidents.
This study suggests that there will be both a new all-time high and a stock market “crash,” 
defined as a loss of 29% or greater before January 2029. A Republican has been elected as of Novem-
ber 5, 2024, and his term will (presumably) last until January 2029.
 The stock market has already fulfilled the first part of this correlation as it is making a new all-
time high. Now we see if it will fulfill the latter part of this study with a decline of at least 29% before 
January 2029.

STOCK SECTORS
Jupiter is in Cancer from June 9, 2025, through June 30, 2026. This will highlight real estate, 
home building, remodeling, weddings, domestic appliances, furniture, restaurants, foods, agricultural 
products, dairy, water supplies, hotels and resorts, and businesses that cater to family activities and 
family planning. Strangely enough, the real estate market began struggling shortly after this transit 
began. It looks like it topped out with Jupiter in early Cancer, and it may bottom in 2027–2028 along 
with the stock market. Jupiter enters Leo from June 30, 2026, through July 26, 2027. This redirects 
attention to companies that cater to parties, social activities, huge events, sports, gambling, risk-
taking, and children.
## Page 110

106
Saturn tends to depress stocks and coincides with cyclical lows in the sectors ruling the sign it 
is in. Saturn is in Pisces from September 1, 2025, to February 14, 2026. But then it finally settles in 
Aries from February 14, 2026, through April 2028. The sign of Aries implies price pressure or lack 
of supplies in the field of military equipment and weapons, defense, sports, athletic equipment and 
apparel, guns, and ammunition. 
However, the ingress of Uranus into Gemini is likely to have a more profound effect on the stock 
market. It entered Gemini first on July 7, 2025. And after a brief return to Taurus, from November 
8, 2025 through April 26, 2026, Uranus will fully re-enter Gemini through August 3, 2032. This is 
a boom-bust period for all sectors related to Gemini. That is, these sectors will often enter a boom 
period for at least 2–5 years during which prices explode to new all-time highs, often appreciating 
4-fold or more from their lows of 2025–2026. After that, they lose about 75–90% of their value by 
the time Uranus enters the next sign. Sectors most prone to this boom-bust cycle in the next six years 
include computers, technology, artificial intelligence, automobiles (electric and driverless), airplanes, 
space exploration, drones, quantum computing, and media companies. It is quite possible that the 
tech-heavy NASDAQ will outperform the DJIA, even with the former being bullish during much of 
this period while the latter is bearish. These are the fields to look for the best investment possibilities, 
but they are also the areas in which bankruptcies are more prone to occur prior to 2032, much like the 
dot-com bubble of 2000–2002. 
CONCLUSIONS
Last year’s book concluded, “Our studies suggest that the stock market is rising to the crest 
of its three-year cycle, ideally due November 2024–July 2025. The ideal price range for this 
crest is approximately 44,000–51,000.” The three-year cycle in the DJIA topped out on Decem-
ber 5, 2024, at 45,059 with a double top of 45,054 on January 31, 2025. Last year’s conclusion 
went on to state, “Once the 3-year cycle crest is completed, a sharp decline (greater than 10%) 
is expected to end by November 2025. Traders and investors are advised to buy that decline in 
anticipation of yet another rally to test or exceed the highs that happened before the decline to 
the 3-year cycle trough.” That also happened with the 3-year cycle low of April 7, in which the 
DJIA fell to 36,611, a drop of 18.74%. It then soared to a new all-time high as this is being writ-
ten, currently challenging 50,000.
For 2026, our forecast calls for the crest of the 18-year cycle to take place at 49,400–57,750, with 
special attention in the zone of 51,609–52,342. This could be achieved prior to the completion of the 
first 50-week cycle, due within 16 weeks of March 27, or within the 2–5 months that follow this low. 
That second high (crest of the second 50-week cycle) could be a double top to the first high, and if so, 
it sets the stage for the beginning of a 37–63% decline due 2028 +/- 1 year. Thus, traders are advised 
to buy the first 50-week cycle trough due within 16 weeks of March 27, 2026, but then look to sell 
the crest of the second 50-week cycle due 2–5 months afterwards.

 THE NASDAQ IN 2026
by Wiebke Held, MMA Analyst
INTRODUCTION
This year, MMA is pleased to provide a yearly outlook on the NASDAQ Composite by MMTA 
Director and MMA Analyst Wiebke Held. Many of the longer-term cycles will match well with those 
of the DJIA, although their actual completions will often be slightly apart from one another in weeks 
or even months.
REVIEW AND PREVIEW
The NASDAQ Composite Index started the year with a retest on January 24, 2025, of the all-time 
high that was printed on December 16, 2024. This all-time high of 20,205 was the 3-year cycle crest 
that formed after a remarkable 100% gain following the lows that formed in October 2022, which 
was the 6-year cycle trough. The retest of the all-time highs occurred again (triple top) on February 
18, which then marked the start of a quick and steep decline into the expected 3-year cycle trough, 
which formed on April 7, 2025, at 14,784. The 3-year cycle trough was followed by an equally steep 
and quick rally with only shallow pullbacks. As expected in the first phases of new cycles, they are 
extremely bullish. And as of this writing, the NASDAQ is still making new highs.
In 2026, we are now reaching the time band for the first 50-week cycle trough within the new 
3-year cycle, which will likely be followed by another rally into the crest of the second 50-week 
phase of the 3-year cycle. But traders and investors must be on the lookout, as this current 3-year 
cycle is the last phase of the current 6- and 9-year cycles, and those are the last phase of the current 
18-year cycle.
With long-term cycles being in their last phase, and intermediate-term cycles entering their sec-
ond phase in 2026, the likelihood of the 18-year crest forming in 2026 is high, which would be the 
start of the decline into the 18-year cycle trough.
For both the long- and intermediate-term cycles analysis, the NASDAQ Composite Index (Ticker: 
IXIC) is used, since this index provides the most historical data available. In the following sections, 
I will refer to the NASDAQ Composite Index as the “NASDAQ.”

The 18-Year Cycle
Since the NASDAQ started trading in 1971, there have been three prominent lows in 1974, 1990, 
and 2009 that suggest an 18-year cycle is present in the NASDAQ. Measured across 100% of the 
instances of the 18-year cycle, its normal length is 17.3 years with an orb of 17 months. Measured 
from its start in March 2009, the NASDAQ will be entering its 17th year of the 18-year cycle in early 
2026. The 18-year cycle trough is due 2024–2027. So as of 2026, we are now in the third year of the 
time band for the 18-year cycle trough. 
There are 3 lows and 2 completed cycles of the 18-year cycle in the history of the NASDAQ so 
far. The past data suggest that the NASDAQ is following the same long-term cycle rhythm as the 
Dow Jones and S&P500 indices. Thus, we use the March 2009 low as the 18-year cycle low even 
though the low in 2002 was lower.
Historically, the 18-year cycle has rallied from its starting low to its crest for 161 months on aver-
age, with a range of 113–180 months before the crest forms. Since March 2009, the NASDAQ has 
rallied for 198 months and is still making new all-time highs as of this writing in November 2025. 
This is the longest period of increase in its history. The appreciation from trough to crest has histori-
cally been 788–1489%, with an average gain of 1139%. The appreciation from the low in March 2009 
until late October 2025 has been over 1680%, again the largest appreciation in its history. Being well 
into the time band for the 18-year cycle trough and seeing an extension beyond the historical bound-
aries of time, going up and appreciation, led me to conclude that the 18-year cycle crest is imminent.
Declines from the crest to the trough have historically lasted 13–108 months with an average of 
61 months. The decline into the 18-year cycle from 1974 to 1990 lasted 13 months, and the decline 
## Page 114

110
into the 18-year cycle from 1990 to 2009 lasted 103 months. If we count the months from the last 
18-year cycle crest in March 2000 to the low in October 2002, the decline lasted 30 months, before a 
double bottom in 2009 stretched this period longer. Hence, one could argue that a more normal length 
of decline into an 18-year cycle trough lasts from 13 to 30 months. The depreciation from the crest to 
the trough has ranged from 34%–75% with an average decline of 55%. 
The current 18-year cycle is breaking down into a combination pattern with lows at the 1/3 
(6-year cycle) and 1/2 marks (9-year cycle). Let’s explore the phases of the 18-year cycle next to 
refine this market timing projection.
The 9-Year Cycle
In the history of the NASDAQ, there are 5 completed instances of the 9-year cycle, which is the 
half-cycle to the 18-year cycle. The 9-year cycle has a mean periodicity of 9.5 years and a normal 
length of 8–11 years. The last 9-year cycle trough happened in March 2020 when the COVID-19 pan-
demic hit, and slightly expanded to 11 years and 1 month. Measured from the March 2020 low, the 
current 9-year cycle is in its 6th year. The next 9-year cycle trough is due between January 2028 and 
April 2031. One may notice that this time band does not overlap with the 18-year cycle time band. 
We at MMA know that cycles tend to balance out over time. Hence, I expect the current 9-year cycle 
to be on the shorter side in length or even contract (6–8 years), as the first 9-year cycle was slightly 
on the longer side and thus expanded somewhat.
The current 9-year cycle is breaking down into a 3-phase pattern with 3-year cycle lows (range 
26–36 months) in October 2022 and April 2025. We are now in the third 3-year cycle which is the 
final phase of the current 9-year cycle, when the low of the 9-year cycle would normally be due. 
Since 1971, all but one 9-year cycle exhibited a right translation, meaning the crest formed 
past the mid-point of the cycle, which is a bullish trend characteristic. Historically, bullish 9-year 
cycles have peaked between 79–132 months with an average of 98 months. As of this writing in 
November 2025, the current 9-year cycle has been going up for 68 months from its start in March 
2020. The appreciation of bullish 9-year cycles has been between 207%–642% with an average of 
421%. Based on this study, the price target for the current 9-year cycle crest is 34,700 with a range 
of 20,500–49,400. The current 9-year cycle has appreciated over 260% so far and is well within 
that range.
The historical range of decline from the crest to trough in bullish 9-year cycles has been 1–15 
months, with an average of 8 months. The historical depreciation in all cases has seen a range of 
29%–75% with an average of 40%. Since we are in the third and final 3-year cycle phase of two 
9-year cycles within the greater 18-year cycle, the next 9-year cycle trough will also be the 18-year 
cycle trough. Thus, we anticipate a 29–75% decline once the crest is in.
The 6-Year Cycle
In the history of the NASDAQ, 8 completed instances of the 6-year cycle can be observed at the 
1/3 intervals of the greater 18-year cycle. The 6-year cycle has a mean periodicity of 5.5 years and a 
normal length of 4–7 years. The last 6-year cycle trough culminated in October 2022. Measured from 
this low, the current 6-year cycle is in its 3rd year. This is the third and final 6-year cycle within the 
current 18-year cycle. 
## Page 115

111
The current 6-year cycle is exhibiting a breakdown into a 2-phase pattern (3-year cycle low in 
April 2025) with bullish characteristics (higher highs and higher lows).
Since 1971, all 6-year cycles exhibited a bullish right translation pattern. Historically, 6-year 
cycles have rallied from trough to crest between 39–76 months with an average of 61 months. As of 
this writing in November 2025, the current 6-year cycle has been going up for 37 months from its 
start in October 2022. The appreciation of 6-year cycles has been between 116%–409% with an aver-
age of 241%. Based on these studies, the price target for the 6-year cycle crest is 34,300 with a range 
of 21,700–51,200. The current 6-year cycle has appreciated over 139% so far and is well within the 
target range already.
The historical range of decline from the crest to trough in all instances of the 6-year cycle has 
been 1–31 months, with an average of 12 months. The historical depreciation has seen a range of 
20%–78% with an average of 38%. Since we are in the third and final of three 6-year cycles within 
the greater 18-year cycle, the next 6-year cycle trough will also be the 9-year cycle and 18-year 
cycle trough. 
Summarizing the long-term cycle review, traders and investors must be alert to the possibility 
of a long-term cycle crest forming at any time now, as the 18-year cycle has already exceeded its 
historical range of time going up and appreciation. Thus, 2026 will likely be the year in which we 
will see the 18-year cycle crest forming. Looking at the sub-cycles of the 18-year cycle, we enter the 
time band for the crest to form within the next 2–11 months, when the 9-year and 6-year cycles start 
to enter their historical ranges. Both cycles have already entered the price target range for their crests. 
As long as price remains above the 22- and 33-month moving average on the monthly chart and 
the market is making new highs, we have not seen the 18-year cycle crest yet. The price target range 
for the crest, where the 9- and 6-year cycle price targets overlap, is 21,700–49,400. Once the crest is 
in, there will be a steep decline into the 18-year cycle trough, which is due in the next 2 years, and 
more specifically, where the time bands of the 18- and 6-year cycles overlap (February 2027–August 
2027). The decline will likely last between 1 and 31 months, with a depreciation of 33%–78% from 
the crest.
INTERMEDIATE-TERM CYCLES
Let’s now further analyze the intermediate-term cycles, as each long-term cycle contains smaller 
sub-cycles (the MMA principle of “cycles within cycles”), enabling us to make more refined market 
timing projections by breaking down and following these sub-cycles and formulate a trading plan for 
2026.
